The entry point detection begins in lib/internal/modules/run_main.js with the shouldUseESMLoader() function (line 64) that determines whether to use the ESM or CJS loader based on file extension and package.json type field. This detection directly influences how modules are loaded at startup.\\n\\nThe core ESM loader is implemented in the ModuleLoader class (lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js, line 110), which orchestrates the entire module loading pipeline. ModuleLoader manages resolution, loading, translation, and job creation through key methods like resolve(), load(), and various utility methods for module registration and caching. The ModuleLoader uses a translators map (defined in lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js, line 81) that contains format-specific module translators including 'module' (standard JS), 'commonjs', 'json', 'builtin', and 'wasm' formats.\\n\\nModule resolution is handled through the ESM specifier resolver, implemented primarily in lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js. The defaultResolve() function (line 1011) handles the resolution of module specifiers to file URLs. Key resolution functions include: moduleResolve() (line 899) for general module path resolution, packageResolve() (line 801) for package.json resolution, packageExportsResolve() (line 588) for handling exports field mapping, and packageImportsResolve() (line 695) for handling imports field mapping. Additional support functions like finalizeResolution() (line 228) and legacyMainResolve() (line 198) complete the resolution pipeline.\\n\\nModule loading is implemented in lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js with defaultLoad() (line 158) and defaultLoadSync() (line 61) handling asynchronous and synchronous module loading respectively. Format detection is handled by lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js which exports defaultGetFormat() (line 240), detectModuleFormat() (line 36), and getFileProtocolModuleFormat() (line 111). Network module fetching is implemented in lib/internal/modules/esm/fetch_module.js with fetchModule() (line 277) and fetchWithRedirects() (line 151).\\n\\nThe ModuleJob class (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js, line 72) represents the linking and evaluation pipeline for a single module. ModuleJob inherits from ModuleJobBase (line 60) and is used for async module loading. A synchronous variant, ModuleJobSync (line 310), handles synchronous module loading for require() in imported CJS modules. The ModuleJob manages the Promise-based evaluation flow and module dependency linking.\\n\\nThe native C++ ModuleWrap binding is implemented in src/module_wrap.cc and src/module_wrap.h. The ModuleWrap class (src/module_wrap.h, line 36) wraps V8 Module objects and provides the bridge between JavaScript and V8's module system. Key methods include Link() (line 470), Instantiate() (line 508), Evaluate() (line 533) for async operations, and their synchronous counterparts InstantiateSync() (line 608) and EvaluateSync() (line 641).
